***lire.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lire.html>lire</a> (12916)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:lire.html>lire</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">lyre</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">līra</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">any fleshy part of the body, muscle, calf of the <a href = vnd.unilang:leg.html>leg</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ligwizô</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*lihwizô</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thigh, groin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*lekʷs-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*lewks-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">groin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">lies</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">groin</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">lår</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thigh</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lire.html>lire</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lires.html>lires</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a>  dialectal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Northern_England" class="extiw" title="w:Northern England">Northern England</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scotland" class="extiw" title="w:Scotland">Scotland</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Flesh, brawn, or muscle; the fleshy part of a person or animal in contradistinction to the bone and skin.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a>  dialectal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scotland" class="extiw" title="w:Scotland">Scotland</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The fleshy part of a roast capon, etc. as distinguished from a limb or joint.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:lire.html>lire</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">lyre</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">hlýr</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cheeks</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, <span class="ann-pos">plural</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:lere.html>lere</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">hlēor</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cheek, countenance, complexion</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:leer.html>leer</a></span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lire.html>lire</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lires.html>lires</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a>  dialectal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scotland" class="extiw" title="w:Scotland">Scotland</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The cheek.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a>  dialectal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scotland" class="extiw" title="w:Scotland">Scotland</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Face; appearance of the face or skin; complexion; hue.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">líri</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">lira</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a>  dialectal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scotland" class="extiw" title="w:Scotland">Scotland</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Orkney" class="extiw" title="w:Orkney">Orkney</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Shetland" class="extiw" title="w:Shetland">Shetland</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> ornithology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The Manx shearwater (bird).</li></ol>

***litanie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:litanie.html>litanie</a> (103615)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">letanie</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">letanīa</i>, older <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">litanīa</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">λιτανεία</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">litaneía</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The classical Latin and Greek forms with <i>li-</i> influenced the current Dutch spelling.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:litanie.html>litanie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:litanie.html>litanieën</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:litanie.html>litanietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>litany <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">liturgical prayer consisting of series of prayers</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr />

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">līturgia</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">λειτουργία</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">leitourgía</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">work in public</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:liturgie.html>liturgie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:liturgie.html>liturgieën</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:liturgie.html>liturgietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A liturgy, predetermined or prescribed set of (religious) rituals and associated customs, attributes etc.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:paus.html>Paus</a> Gregorius <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:grote.html>Grote</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deed.html>deed</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>veel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> uniformizering <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:katholieke.html>Katholieke</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:liturgie.html>liturgie</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:inclusief.html>inclusief</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verplicht.html>verplicht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gebruik.html>gebruik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Latijnse teksen</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Pope Gregory the Great <a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>did</a> a lot to uniformize the Catholic liturgy, including the obligatory use of Latin texts</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>A liturgy, a booklet with <a href = vnd.unilang:details.html>details</a> about the <a href = vnd.unilang:songs.html>songs</a> sung and texts read in a mass or other religious service.</li>
<li>A liturgy, Ancient Greek service to the public interest</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">liturg</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">liturgiek</span></li>

<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lobbes.html>lobbes</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lobbes.html>lobbesen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lobbes.html>lobbesje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">endearing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> large, well-mannered or friendly dog</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">endearing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> kindly but oafish person</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lobje.html>lobje</a> (115565)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">lubben</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">lib</i>. <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> missing or incomplete. <hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:lobje.html>lobje</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to castrate, neuter, <a href = vnd.unilang:geld.html>geld</a></li>
<li>to jerk off</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">lobotomy</i>, coined by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Walter_Jackson_Freeman_II" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Walter Jackson Freeman II"><a href = vnd.unilang:walter.html>Walter</a> Jackson Freeman II</a>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">λοβός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lobós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lobe (of the brain)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">τομή</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tomḗ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cut, slice</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***locomotief.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:locomotief.html>locomotief</a> (16232)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">locomotive</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:locomotief.html>locomotief</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:locomotieven.html>locomotieven</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:locomotief.html>locomotiefje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>locomotive, self-propelled vehicle that <a href = vnd.unilang:runs.html>runs</a> on <a href = vnd.unilang:rails.html>rails</a>, notably pulling a train
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">treintrekker</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">diesellocomotief</span></li>

***loeder.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:loeder.html>loeder</a> (21035)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:loeder.html>loeder</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bait, lure</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The relatively recent, mostly postwar shift toward denoting females in particular may be inspired by its cognate <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Luder</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">slut</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Also cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">lure</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:loeder.html>loeder</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:loeders.html>loeders</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:loeder.html>loedertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A nasty person or animal.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">offensive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> now especially</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <a href = vnd.unilang:bitch.html>bitch</a>, a nasty woman (or female animal).</li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:gemeen.html>gemeen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:persoon.html>persoon</a>

***loef.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:loef.html>loef</a> (51381)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">*<a href = vnd.unilang:loef.html>loef</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*luof</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*lōf-</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*lāp-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*lēp-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*lep-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:flat.html>flat</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>Although attested only very late, its origin in Old Dutch <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> relatively certain as Old French borrowed <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro"><a href = vnd.unilang:lof.html>lof</a></i> from it.
</p><p>Cognate, with various inflectional variants, with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml">lōf</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">lōf</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">lófi</i>, Gothic <i class="Goth mention" lang="got">𐌻𐍉𐍆𐌰</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="got-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lōfa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. With a prefix also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">glove</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">glófi</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:loef.html>loef</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:loeven.html>loeven</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:loef.html>loefje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">luff</span>, windward side of a sail or ship. (no plural)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Originally, an obscure <span class="Latn" lang="en">nautical</span> device <a href = vnd.unilang:turned.html>turned</a> to change a sailing ship’s course.</li></ol>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:loef.html>loef</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:loeven.html>loeven</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:loef.html>loefje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>(<i>This sense might have a different etymology</i>) A sawn-out cavity in one of two crossing pieces of wood in which the other locks</li></ol>

<p>Germanic, uncertain
</p>

***loeren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:loeren.html>loeren</a> (21878)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>With dialectal (eastern) <i>-oe-</i> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:luren.html>luren</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to look sharp</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">lauern</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">lour</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lurken.html>lurk</a></i>.
</p>

<p>Since 1779. ***lol.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lol.html>lol</a> (1239)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span></h3>
<p>Of uncertain origin. Found in publications from as early as 1560. Probably derived from the onomatopoeia <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">lollen</i>, originally meaning 'to snooze'. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">loll</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lol.html>lol</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:lolletje.html>lolletje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>fun
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wij.html>Wij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:veel.html>veel</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lol.html>lol</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> are having a lot of fun.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>Wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lol.html>lol</a>!</b></i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">What a laugh!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>2012</b>, Raymond Klompsma amp; Stefan Wobben, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:zo.html>Zo</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a>: websites <a href = vnd.unilang:ontwerp.html>ontwerp</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mensen.html>mensen</a></i>, Concept7, page 25:
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>Dit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mensen.html>mensen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:graag.html>graag</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:lol.html>lol</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:leven.html>leven</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:prettig.html>prettig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:willen.html>willen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voelen.html>voelen</a>.
<dl><dd>These are people who like to have <b>fun</b> in their <a href = vnd.unilang:lives.html>lives</a>, who want to feel good.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li>

***lollipop.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:lollipop.html>lollipop</a> (68962)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Multiple <a href = vnd.unilang:theories.html>theories</a> abound. One <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> that it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Angloromani_language" class="extiw" title="w:Angloromani language">Angloromani</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="rme">lollipobbul</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">candy apple</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Another <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> that it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> derived from <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">loll</i> ("to dangle the tongue") + <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">pop</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lollipop.html>lollipop</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">lollipops</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>An item of confectionery consisting of a piece of candy/sweet attached to a stick.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lolly.html>lolly</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">sucker</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">US</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ul>
